<h1 _ngcontent-nyd-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="loginComponentManager (华为账号登录组件管理)"> loginComponentManager (华为账号登录组件管理) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供华为账号登录组件的逻辑管理，辅助应用通过集成华为账号登录组件完成登录功能。</p>    <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="section16609101116259" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section16609101116259" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-nyd-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { loginComponentManager } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.AccountKit'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1316px;">     <h2 id="section79023235528" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv">LoginType<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section79023235528" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>该枚举定义了华为账号登录类型。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AuthenticationServices.HuaweiID.UIComponent</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.4.1.1" width="31.64%">          <p>名称</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.4.1.2" width="10.489999999999998%">          <p>值</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.4.1.3" width="57.87%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.64%">          <p>ID</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.489999999999998%">          <p>0</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="57.87%">          <p>表示用OpenID、UnionID来关联华为账号。</p>          <p>用户在登录成功后会返回对应数据。</p>          <p>该登录类型响应数据包含openID、unionID、authorizationCode、idToken字段。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.64%">          <p>PHONE_NUMBER</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.489999999999998%">          <p>1</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="57.87%">          <p>表示用PhoneNumber来关联华为账号。</p>          <p>用户在登录成功后，如之前未对快速验证手机号进行授权，则会拉起手机号授权页面；如已授权，则返回对应数据。</p>          <p>该登录类型不需要实时验证华为账号的手机号码，响应数据包含openID、unionID、authorizationCode、idToken字段。</p>          <p>应用使用Authorization Code调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-obtain-user-token#section1085901313579">获取用户级凭证接口</a>向华为账号服务器请求获取Access Token，再使用Access Token调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-get-user-info-get-phone#section2520125725115">获取华为账号用户信息接口</a>获取用户信息，从用户信息中获取用户手机号。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.64%">          <p>REAL_TIME_PHONE_NUMBER</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.489999999999998%">          <p>2</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="57.87%">          <p>表示用PhoneNumber来关联华为账号。</p>          <p>用户每次在登录成功后，都会拉起实时验证手机号授权页面。</p>          <p>该登录类型会实时验证华为账号的手机号码，响应数据包含openID、unionID、authorizationCode、idToken字段。</p>          <p>应用使用Authorization Code调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-obtain-user-token#section1085901313579">获取用户级凭证接口</a>向华为账号服务器请求获取Access Token，再使用Access Token调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-get-user-info-get-phone#section2520125725115">获取华为账号用户信息接口</a>获取用户信息，从用户信息中获取用户手机号。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>REAL_TIME_PHONE_NUMBER暂不支持使用。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.64%">          <p>QUICK_LOGIN</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.489999999999998%">          <p>3</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="57.87%">          <p>表示用PhoneNumber来关联华为账号。</p>          <p>该类型不支持Icon类型和图文类型的LoginWithHuaweiIDButton组件。</p>          <p>该登录类型需要通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-authentication#section12940173017165">AuthorizationWithHuaweiIDRequest</a>接口获取华为账号绑定的匿名手机号，如果未获取到华为账号绑定的匿名手机号，请使用其他登录类型。</p>          <p>该登录类型响应数据包含openID、unionID、authorizationCode、idToken字段。</p>          <p>应用使用Authorization Code调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-get-user-info-quicklogin-by-code#section2520125725115">/oauth2/v6/quickLogin/getPhoneNumber接口</a>获取用户信息，从用户信息中获取用户手机号。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>          <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、PC/2in1、Tablet、TV(仅在5.1.1版本)中可正常调用，在其他设备类型中返回1001500003错误码。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 831px;">     <h2 id="section52091116105916" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv">AppInfo<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AuthenticationServices.HuaweiID.UIComponent</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.6.1.1" width="16.259999999999998%"> <p>appIcon</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="21.01%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" <p>应用的图标。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="16.259999999999998%">          <p>appName</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="21.01%">          <p><a <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.26%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p>应用的名称，长度限制1-19个字符，字符超长和大字体下展示不全会截断，使用省略号填充。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="16.259999999999998%">          <p>appDescription</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="21.01%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr" target="_blank">ResourceStr</a></p></td>         <td <p>应用的详细描述，长度限制1-44个字符。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <ul>             <li>在4.1.0(11)版本，为必填参数。</li> </div></div></div></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 522px;">     <h2 id="section7401948625" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv">TextType<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section7401948625" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>该枚举定义了显示在登录面板上的隐私文本类型。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AuthenticationServices.HuaweiID.UIComponent</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.6.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%"> id="mcps1.3.6.6.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>PLAIN_TEXT</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>0</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>纯文本类型不支持点击。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>RICH_TEXT</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>1</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>富文本类型展示为蓝色，支持点击。用于展示《华为账号用户认证协议》和应用相关隐私协议。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 663px;">     <h2 id="section7272252193" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv">PrivacyText<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section7272252193" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>该接口定义了使用登录面板或登录按钮时需要展示的隐私文本。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AuthenticationServices.HuaweiID.UIComponent</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.6.1.1" width="14.56%">          <p>名称</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.6.1.2" width="14.530000000000001%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.6.1.3" width="20.200000000000003%">          <p>只读</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.6.1.4" width="17.89%">          <p>可选</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.6.1.5" width="32.82%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.56%">          <p>type</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.530000000000001%">          <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section7401948625">TextType</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.200000000000003%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.89%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p>隐私文本的类型，包含纯文本和富文本。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.56%">          <p>text</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.530000000000001%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr" target="_blank">ResourceStr</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.200000000000003%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.89%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p>在登录面板上显示的隐私文本内容，一般用于展示应用隐私协议和《华为账号用户认证协议》跳转链接。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.56%">          <p>tag</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.530000000000001%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.200000000000003%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.89%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p>当type类型为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section7401948625">TextType.RICH_TEXT</a>必须设置tag。当用户点击文本时将跳转应用给tag设置的链接，应用可以根据用户的点击行为展示不同的隐私内容。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 570px;">     <h2 id="section1248254952118" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv">LoginIcon<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>该接口定义了可选登录区域展示的登录Icon属性。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AuthenticationServices.HuaweiID.UIComponent</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.6.1.6.1.1" width="19.15%">   <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.72%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">PixelMap</a> | <a device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv">HuaweiIDCredential<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AuthenticationServices.HuaweiID.UIComponent</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p> width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>unionID</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="11.76%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.200000000000003%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.89%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p><span style="color: rgb(53,53,53);">UnionID。</span><span style="color: rgb(53,53,53);">UnionID是华为账号用户在同一个开发者账号下产品的身份ID</span>，同一个用户，<span style="color: rgb(53,53,53);">同一个开发者账号下</span>管理的不同应用，UnionID值相同。具体格式要求请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/account-faq-9" target="_blank">OpenID和UnionID的格式说明</a>。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder"       <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.89%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p><span style="color: rgb(53,53,53);">OpenID。OpenID</span><span style="color: rgb(53,53,53);">是华为账号用户在不同类型的产品的身份ID</span>，同一个用户，不同应用，OpenID值不同。具体格式要求请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/account-faq-9" target="_blank">OpenID和UnionID的格式说明</a>。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>authorizationCode</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="11.76%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.200000000000003%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.89%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p>Authorization Code。临时凭据，用于获取Access Token，有效时间5分钟，并且只能使用1次。长度限制1-1024。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>idToken</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="11.76%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.200000000000003%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.89%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p>ID Token。JWT格式的字符串，包含用户信息，用于应用获取部分用户相关信息及验证签名。长度限制1-2048。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>enableSecurityVerification</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="11.76%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.200000000000003%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.89%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.82%">          <p>enableSecurityVerification。华为账号用户是否开启一键登录增强身份验证。如果开发者需要获取该字段，请将参数<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section4717249182518">securityVerification</a>设置为false。</p>          <p>仅登录类型为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section79023235528">LoginType.QUICK_LOGIN</a>时会返回该字段。</p>          <p>true：表示用户已启用增强身份验证。</p>          <p>false：表示用户未启用增强身份验证。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>6.0.0(20)</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>verifyPhoneNumber</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.75%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="18.23%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="16.86%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.83%">          <p>华为账号用户在过去90天内未进行短信验证，是否拉起Account Kit提供的短信验证码页面。</p>          <p>true：拉起Account Kit提供的短信验证码页面。</p>          <p>false：不拉起Account Kit提供的短信验证码页面。需要应用验证手机号时效性。</p>          <p>默认值：true。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>extraStyle</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.75%">          <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section87572031102713">ExtraStyle</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="18.23%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="16.86%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.83%">          <p>如果应用想使用华为账号提供的固定样式之外的效果，可使用此接口自定义按钮样式。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>loginButtonTextType</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.75%">          <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section1645283915811">LoginButtonTextType</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="18.23%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="16.86%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.83%">          <p>当loginType为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section79023235528">LoginType.QUICK_LOGIN</a>时，可传入此参数，控制按钮文本内容显示。</p>          <p>默认值：<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section1645283915811">LoginButtonTextType.QUICK_LOGIN</a></p>          <ul>           <li>当该参数为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section1645283915811">LoginButtonTextType.QUICK_LOGIN</a>时，按钮文本内容显示“华为账号一键登录”。</li>           <li>当该参数为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section1645283915811">LoginButtonTextType.QUICK_REGISTRATION</a>时，按钮文本内容显示“华为账号一键注册”。</li>          </ul>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>riskLevel</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.75%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="18.23%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="16.86%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.83%">          <p>是否需要获取华为账号用户风险等级。</p>          <p>仅登录类型为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section79023235528">LoginType.QUICK_LOGIN</a>时需要设置该参数。</p>          <p>true：需要<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/account-get-risklevel-byquicklogin" target="_blank">获取用户风险等级</a>。</p>          <p>false：不获取用户风险等级。</p>          <p>默认值：false。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.330000000000002%">          <p>securityVerification</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.75%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="18.23%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="16.86%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.83%">          <p>用户开启华为账号一键登录增强身份验证后，应用会在登录过程中通过华为账号使用生物识别或短信进行身份验证。如果需要获取用户一键登录增强身份验证的开关状态，需设置该字段为false。</p>          <p>仅登录类型为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section79023235528">LoginType.QUICK_LOGIN</a>时需要设置该参数。</p>          <p>true：响应结果HuaweiIDCredential将不会返回 <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section1862534912215">enableSecurityVerification</a>。</p>          <p>默认值：true。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>6.0.0(20)</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2159px;">     <h2 <p>当rotation的数据类型为string时，合法的取值为纯数字或纯数字后带"deg"(度)、"rad"(弧度)、"grad"(梯度)、"turn"(圈)单位，例如："90"、 "90deg"、"1.57rad"。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12.18%"> <h2 id="section4742141694510" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv">ButtonStyle<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section4742141694510" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>该类定义了华为账号登录按钮的通用属性。通过new loginComponentManager.ButtonStyle()构造实例。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AuthenticationServices.HuaweiID.UIComponent</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 992px;">     <h3 id="section13497267017" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,tv" class="firsth2">buttonSize<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section13497267017" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span></div><p>buttonSize(value: ButtonSize): ButtonStyle</p>     <p>调用该方法设置华为账号登录按钮的宽高尺寸。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong><strong>：</strong>SystemCapability.AuthenticationServices.HuaweiID.UIComponent</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.8.1.5.1.1" width="10.530000000000001%">          <p>参数名</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.8.1.5.1.2" width="17.810000000000002%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.8.1.5.1.3" width="28.93%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.8.1.5.1.4" width="42.730000000000004%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.530000000000001%">          <p>value</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.810000000000002%">          <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section169691441164919">ButtonSize</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.93%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="42.730000000000004%">          <p>当按钮类型为纯图标按钮时，按钮的宽度和高度相等，取value.width和value.height的非undefined的最小值，如果value.width和value.height都为undefined取<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/account-api-component-manager#section4717249182518">LoginWithHuaweiIDButtonParams</a>的iconRadius的2倍值，如果iconRadius也是undefined则取默认值48vp；</p>          <p>当按钮类型为非纯图标按钮时，按钮的宽度和高度分别取value.width和value.height，当value.width或者value.height为undefined，按钮宽度或高度取父布局宽高。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip warn"><div class="title">注意</div><div class="content">            <p>当设置该属性的宽高，父组件的宽高值应该大于等于该属性的宽高值。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p> LoginWithHuaweiIDButtonController</p>     <p>华为账号登录按钮的点击事件。使用callback异步回调。应用可以在用户点击华为账号登录按钮后收到回调，可用于记录运营事件等场景。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>
